typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>03.29.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/brigidaguerreiro\">Brígida Lourenço Guerreiro</a> and the folks over at <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/kobuagency\">KOBU Agency</a> shared a really cool 3D project exploring glass texture and typography. The project from my understanding was created to celebrate KOBU Foundry’s first anniversary. As they shared in the description, building a type foundry within a creative agency is not very usual in Portugal and they had the opportunity to embark on such an adventure by mid-December 2018 and carry on the task to emphasise the importance of this pillar in graphic design. The whole project was created using Blender 3D.</p>\n\n<p><img src=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/OpCaerjXCfo-elWQ9ceVAWsUe3mYf11tkfgehZFNhmzfUpKom5IALJCZwf9OPfaQyE_ITglLmu21XPUhZ5xNDX8-f1B9G9nInVWfAYuvwc50iNOCzBLhAiEFMT24HLYb6upNSqF0\" Let's all take a closer look!</p>\n\n<p>In their words</p>\n\n<p>TECH4ALL is a digital inclusion initiative supported by the Chinese technology company Huawei, which approached us to help them present how technology significantly improves the quality of life in four particular fields: education, health, environment, and development.</p>\n\n<p>The main hero, a metaphor for technology, takes us to an African Savannah, a hospital, a rainforest, and a remote little village and transmutes people’s life: provides kids with new digital skills, improves the standard of the health care, protects the environment, drives balanced development. company called HyperCommute. The project was part of an interview process, but for me what is more important to highlight it is the step by step design process, from problem definition, references/inspiration, concepts to the final solution. On top of that, the whole presentation has an impeccable visual design, which highlights the Braz specialization in branding, marketing and more traditional graphic design work. href=\"https://www.behance.net/andreiongd\">Andreion de Castro</a> shared a motion design post where he plays with typography and movement. \"POEMS: VOLUME II\" is a collection of quotes and lyrics taken from a range of songs and movies inspired by Andreion’s taste in music and cinema. “My intent with the animations is to evoke emotions and feelings; Something we can perhaps resonate with.” </p>\n\n<p>Lyrics taken from Daniel Caesar, Sufjan Stevens, Frank Ocean, Audrey Hepburn, Tame Impala amongst many others. All coded using Processing. Today, we are proud to <a href=\"https://apps.apple.com/us/app/abdz-do/id1555948560\">introduce our iOS app</a>. For this post I wanted to share some photos from a series called Harbour Hamburg II. class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/___debut___\">DEBUT's design</a> team shared a beautiful branding and visual identity project for Alive Parts. With the motto “We believe technology is at its best when it feels alive”, the designers from DEBUT looked from inspiration in the 80s, my favorite decade and by now you know where this is going. The clever idea of making two letters with pixelated parts was genius in my opinion and kept the ID fresh but still with that retro feel. </p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img alt=\"Image may
